(S.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  [Hence,] <hi rend="ital">He gained, acquired,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">earned,</hi> wealth or the like; as also

                  <hi rend="ital">he applied himself, as to a task, to gain, &amp;c.</hi> (S.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">كَسَبَ</foreign> is also said to signify, and originally, both <hi rend="ital">he sought,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">sought after,</hi> [<hi rend="ital">sustenance</hi>]; and <hi rend="ital">he laboured in seeking,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">seeking after, sustenance.</hi> (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="5">-b5-</sense>

(IJ.) (A.)          <sense type="b" n="6">-b6-</sense>  [This distinction, however, is not always observed: for] <foreign lang="ar">كَسَبَ</foreign> signifies, <hi rend="ital">He did</hi> either a good or an evil deed: [because he who does so earns, or draws upon himself, reward or punishment.] (Jel in ii. 281; and iii. 24; &amp;c.)                   </form> The <hi rend="ital">wolf.</hi> (L, K.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">A name of a bitch:</hi> (S:) <hi rend="ital">one of the names of the bitch:</hi> (ISd:) as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n36932-1" target="كَسْبَةُ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n36929"/></foreign>: (K:) as   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n36932-2" target="كُسَيْبٌ" n="2" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n36934"/></foreign> is <hi rend="ital">a name of the dog;</hi> i. e., of the male: (K:) names thus used as ominous of gain, [or of capturing game]: (IM:) <foreign lang="ar">كَسَابِ</foreign>, as <hi rend="ital">a name of a hunting bitch,</hi> means <foreign lang="ar">كَاسِبَةٌ</foreign>.
